POLITICAL
Reported Replacement of "Front Hati val" by a New Paper
The following report is from a member of the staff of "Front
National" and is a close friend of Theret. This information was disclosed
directly to a well-tried source, who has extensive contacts in French press
circuless
1. It appears improbable that "Front Nationel" will continue
to be published after the collections, because of the brecking down of this po-
titional formation, which in of no further interest - exempt perhaps a marpi-
nal one - to the Consultant Farty. However, until nor, Thoree has been oppo-
sed to its disapparance.
2. At present the leaders of the 3P are planning to rep lase
it by a more effective origin, and are studying three possible solutions
(a) A newspaper which might be called "The Matin", and which
would be supplementary to "The Solt" which would be responsible for the publi-
ation. The directors of "The Solt", which is a successful paper, are opposed
to this idea, because they do not see the necessity for placing an additional
load on the business.
(b) A paper exclusively for known and which would treat all
questions interesting to moment the home, the factory, foci, the ohld, ele-
thing, education, eda. But it is wondered if women have not noted the ha-
bit of reading their kuebards' paper, and would not be reluctant to indulge
in the equina of an extra paper.
(c) An evening "Your which would sell for 3 fr, and which
would be a sinil of the "The Solt" in form, and would be the leclet opposite
number of "Int paper. This paper would be destined primarily for the elite,
and would stress cultural mitter, accurate, documentation, etc. The official-
ty lies in assembling a first nite editorial staff to handle the political,
sconnatic, financial and artistic departments of such A paper.
3. It appears likely that a decision will be resolved before
the end of May,
